ARQUIVO: C:\Users\Alex Salles\Apps - desenvolvimento\petjoy_app\firestore.rules
==================================================
   1: rules_version = '2';
   2: service cloud.firestore {
   3:   match /databases/{database}/documents {
   4:     function isMaster() {
   5:       return request.auth != null &&
   6:         get(/databases/$(database)/documents/users/$(request.auth.uid)).data.role == 'master';
   7:     }
   8:     match /products/{id} {
   9:       allow read: if true;
  10:       allow create, update, delete: if isMaster();
  11:     }
  12:     match /settings/{docId} {
  13:   		allow read, write: if isMaster();
  14: 		}
  15:     match /users/{userId} {
  16:       allow get: if request.auth != null && (request.auth.uid == userId || isMaster());
  17:       allow list: if request.auth != null;
  18:       allow create: if request.auth != null && request.auth.uid == userId;
  19:       allow update: if isMaster();
  20:     }
  21:     match /orders/{orderId} {
  22:       allow read: if request.auth != null &&
  23:         (request.auth.uid == resource.data.customerId || isMaster());
  24:       allow create: if request.auth != null &&
  25:         request.auth.uid == request.resource.data.customerId &&
  26:         request.resource.data.status == 'awaiting_payment' &&
  27:         request.resource.data.total is number &&
  28:         request.resource.data.total > 0;
  29:       allow update: if isMaster();
  30:     }
  31:   }
  32: }

ARQUIVO: C:\Users\Alex Salles\Apps - desenvolvimento\petjoy_app\importar_produtos.js
==================================================
   1: /**
   2:  * importar_produtos.js
   3:  *
   4:  * Importa produtos de uma planilha Excel para o Firestore.
   5:  * Evita duplicatas: se o produto já existir (mesmo nome + quantidade),
   6:  * atualiza o preço. Se não existir, cria.
   7:  *
   8:  * USO:
   9:  *   node importar_produtos.js                        <- usa Lista_de_produtos.xlsx
  10:  *   node importar_produtos.js outra_planilha.xlsx    <- usa outro arquivo
  11:  *
  12:  * FORMATO ESPERADO DA PLANILHA:
  13:  *   Coluna B: Nome do produto
  14:  *   Coluna C: Quantidade (ex: 250g, 100g, 50g)
  15:  *   Coluna D: Preço (número)
  16:  *   Coluna E: Animal (cachorro | gato | ambos)
  17:  *   Linha 1: ignorada (cabeçalho ou vazia)
  18:  *   Linha 2: cabeçalho (Nome, Quantity, Preço, Animal) — ignorada
  19:  *   A partir da linha 3: dados
  20:  */
  21: 
  22: const admin = require('firebase-admin');
  23: const XLSX = require('xlsx');
  24: const path = require('path');
  25: 
  26: // ---- Configuração ----
  27: const SERVICE_ACCOUNT_PATH = path.join(__dirname, 'serviceAccountKeyPetJoy.json');
  28: const ARQUIVO_XLSX = process.argv[2] || 'Lista_de_produtos.xlsx';
  29: 
  30: // ---- Inicializa Firebase ----
  31: const serviceAccount = require(SERVICE_ACCOUNT_PATH);
  32: 
  33: admin.initializeApp({
  34:   credential: admin.credential.cert(serviceAccount),
  35: });
  36: 
  37: const db = admin.firestore();
  38: 
  39: // ---- Lê a planilha ----
  40: function lerPlanilha(caminho) {
  41:   const wb = XLSX.readFile(caminho);
  42:   const ws = wb.Sheets[wb.SheetNames[0]];
  43:   const rows = XLSX.utils.sheet_to_json(ws, { header: 1, defval: null });
  44: 
  45:   const produtos = [];
  46: 
  47:   // Linha 0 = vazia, linha 1 = cabeçalho → começa na linha 2 (índice 2)
  48:   for (let i = 2; i < rows.length; i++) {
  49:     const row = rows[i];
  50: 
  51:     // Colunas: A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3, E=4
  52:     const nome = (row[1] || '').toString().trim();
  53:     const quantidade = (row[2] || '').toString().trim();
  54:     const preco = parseFloat(row[3]) || 0;
  55:     const animal = (row[4] || '').toString().trim().toLowerCase();
  56: 
  57:     if (!nome || preco === 0) continue;
  58: 
  59:     produtos.push({ nome, quantidade, preco, animal });
  60:   }
  61: 
  62:   return produtos;
  63: }
  64: 
  65: // ---- Mapeia animal para categoria legível ----
  66: function mapearCategoria(animal) {
  67:   switch (animal) {
  68:     case 'cachorro': return 'Cachorro';
  69:     case 'gato':     return 'Gato';
  70:     case 'ambos':    return 'Ambos';
  71:     default:         return animal || 'Geral';
  72:   }
  73: }
  74: 
  75: // ---- Importa para o Firestore ----
  76: async function importar(produtos) {
  77:   const colecao = db.collection('products');
  78:   let criados = 0;
  79:   let atualizados = 0;
  80:   let erros = 0;
  81: 
  82:   for (const p of produtos) {
  83:     try {
  84:       const descricao = p.quantidade ? `Embalagem: ${p.quantidade}` : '';
  85:       const categoria = mapearCategoria(p.animal);
  86: 
  87:       // Chave de deduplicação: nome + quantidade
  88:       const snapshot = await colecao
  89:         .where('name', '==', p.nome)
  90:         .where('description', '==', descricao)
  91:         .limit(1)
  92:         .get();
  93: 
  94:       const agora = admin.firestore.FieldValue.serverTimestamp();
  95: 
  96:       if (!snapshot.empty) {
  97:         // Atualiza preço e categoria se o produto já existir
  98:         await snapshot.docs[0].ref.update({
  99:           price: p.preco,
 100:           category: categoria,
 101:           updatedAt: agora,
 102:         });
 103:         console.log(`  ✏️  Atualizado: ${p.nome} (${p.quantidade}) → R$ ${p.preco.toFixed(2)}`);
 104:         atualizados++;
 105:       } else {
 106:         // Cria novo produto
 107:         await colecao.add({
 108:           name: p.nome,
 109:           description: descricao,
 110:           price: p.preco,
 111:           category: categoria,
 112:           imageUrl: '',
 113:           isActive: true,
 114:           isFeatured: false,
 115:           createdAt: agora,
 116:           updatedAt: agora,
 117:         });
 118:         console.log(`  ✅  Criado:     ${p.nome} (${p.quantidade}) → R$ ${p.preco.toFixed(2)}`);
 119:         criados++;
 120:       }
 121:     } catch (err) {
 122:       console.error(`  ❌  Erro em "${p.nome}": ${err.message}`);
 123:       erros++;
 124:     }
 125:   }
 126: 
 127:   return { criados, atualizados, erros };
 128: }
 129: 
 130: // ---- Execução principal ----
 131: (async () => {
 132:   const caminhoArquivo = path.join(__dirname, ARQUIVO_XLSX);
 133: 
 134:   console.log(`\nNatural PetJoy — Importador de Produtos`);
 135:   console.log(`Arquivo: ${caminhoArquivo}\n`);
 136: 
 137:   let produtos;
 138:   try {
 139:     produtos = lerPlanilha(caminhoArquivo);
 140:   } catch (err) {
 141:     console.error(`Erro ao ler planilha: ${err.message}`);
 142:     process.exit(1);
 143:   }
 144: 
 145:   if (produtos.length === 0) {
 146:     console.log('Nenhum produto encontrado na planilha.');
 147:     process.exit(0);
 148:   }
 149: 
 150:   console.log(`${produtos.length} produto(s) encontrado(s). Importando...\n`);
 151: 
 152:   const { criados, atualizados, erros } = await importar(produtos);
 153: 
 154:   console.log(`\n─────────────────────────────`);
 155:   console.log(`  Criados:    ${criados}`);
 156:   console.log(`  Atualizados: ${atualizados}`);
 157:   console.log(`  Erros:      ${erros}`);
 158:   console.log(`─────────────────────────────\n`);
 159: 
 160:   process.exit(erros > 0 ? 1 : 0);
 161: })();

ARQUIVO: C:\Users\Alex Salles\Apps - desenvolvimento\petjoy_app\functions\index.js
==================================================
   1: /**
   2:  * Cloud Functions — Natural PetJoy
   3:  *
   4:  * Funções:
   5:  *   criarPagamentoPix  — callable — cria pagamento Pix no Mercado Pago
   6:  *   webhookMercadoPago — HTTPS   — recebe notificações de pagamento do MP
   7:  *
   8:  * Setup inicial (executar UMA VEZ no terminal):
   9:  *   firebase functions:secrets:set MERCADOPAGO_ACCESS_TOKEN
  10:  *   (cole o Access Token quando solicitado)
  11:  *
  12:  * Deploy:
  13:  *   firebase deploy --only functions
  14:  */
  15: 
  16: "use strict";
  17: 
  18: const { setGlobalOptions } = require("firebase-functions/v2");
  19: const { onCall, onRequest, HttpsError } = require("firebase-functions/v2/https");
  20: const { defineSecret } = require("firebase-functions/params");
  21: const { initializeApp } = require("firebase-admin/app");
  22: const { getFirestore, FieldValue } = require("firebase-admin/firestore");
  23: const https = require("https");
  24: 
  25: initializeApp();
  26: 
  27: setGlobalOptions({
  28:   region: "southamerica-east1",
  29:   maxInstances: 10,
  30: });
  31: 
  32: // Secret Manager — token nunca fica exposto no código ou no Firestore
  33: const mpAccessToken = defineSecret("MERCADOPAGO_ACCESS_TOKEN");
  34: 
  35: // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  36: // Utilitários
  37: // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  38: 
  39: /**
  40:  * Faz uma requisição HTTPS e retorna { statusCode, body (objeto parseado) }.
  41:  */
  42: function mpRequest({ method, path, body, token }) {
  43:   return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
  44:     const payload = body ? JSON.stringify(body) : null;
  45:     const options = {
  46:       hostname: "api.mercadopago.com",
  47:       path,
  48:       method,
  49:       headers: {
  50:         "Content-Type": "application/json",
  51:         Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`,
  52:         "X-Idempotency-Key": body?.external_reference ?? Date.now().toString(),
  53:       },
  54:     };
  55:     if (payload) {
  56:       options.headers["Content-Length"] = Buffer.byteLength(payload);
  57:     }
  58: 
  59:     const req = https.request(options, (res) => {
  60:       let raw = "";
  61:       res.on("data", (chunk) => (raw += chunk));
  62:       res.on("end", () => {
  63:         try {
  64:           resolve({ statusCode: res.statusCode, body: JSON.parse(raw) });
  65:         } catch {
  66:           resolve({ statusCode: res.statusCode, body: raw });
  67:         }
  68:       });
  69:     });
  70: 
  71:     req.on("error", reject);
  72:     if (payload) req.write(payload);
  73:     req.end();
  74:   });
  75: }
  76: 
  77: /**
  78:  * Lê a configuração do Mercado Pago salva no Firestore (sandbox flag).
  79:  * O accessToken vem exclusivamente do Secret Manager.
  80:  */
  81: async function getMpConfig(db) {
  82:   const doc = await db.collection("settings").doc("mercadopago").get();
  83:   if (!doc.exists) return { sandbox: true };
  84:   return doc.data();
  85: }
  86: 
  87: // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  88: // criarPagamentoPix
  89: // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  90: 
  91: exports.criarPagamentoPix = onCall(
  92:   {
  93:     secrets: [mpAccessToken],
  94:     enforceAppCheck: false, // habilite após configurar App Check
  95:   },
  96:   async (request) => {
  97:     // 1. Autenticação
  98:     if (!request.auth) {
  99:       throw new HttpsError("unauthenticated", "Usuário não autenticado.");
 100:     }
 101: 
 102:     const { orderId, total, customerEmail, customerName } = request.data;
 103: 
 104:     if (!orderId || !total || !customerEmail || !customerName) {
 105:       throw new HttpsError("invalid-argument", "Parâmetros obrigatórios ausentes.");
 106:     }
 107: 
 108:     const db = getFirestore();
 109:     const token = mpAccessToken.value();
 110: 
 111:     if (!token) {
 112:       throw new HttpsError(
 113:         "failed-precondition",
 114:         "Token do Mercado Pago não configurado. Configure o secret MERCADOPAGO_ACCESS_TOKEN."
 115:       );
 116:     }
 117: 
 118:     // 2. Verifica se o pedido existe e pertence ao usuário
 119:     const orderRef = db.collection("orders").doc(orderId);
 120:     const orderSnap = await orderRef.get();
 121: 
 122:     if (!orderSnap.exists) {
 123:       throw new HttpsError("not-found", "Pedido não encontrado.");
 124:     }
 125: 
 126:     const orderData = orderSnap.data();
 127:     if (orderData.customerId !== request.auth.uid) {
 128:       throw new HttpsError("permission-denied", "Acesso negado.");
 129:     }
 130: 
 131:     // 3. Lê configuração (sandbox)
 132:     const config = await getMpConfig(db);
 133: 
 134:     // 4. Cria pagamento Pix no Mercado Pago
 135:     const paymentBody = {
 136:       transaction_amount: Number(total.toFixed(2)),
 137:       description: `Pedido Natural PetJoy #${orderId.substring(0, 8).toUpperCase()}`,
 138:       payment_method_id: "pix",
 139:       external_reference: orderId,
 140:       notification_url: "https://webhookmercadopago-klxlcaoqfq-rj.a.run.app",
 141:       payer: {
 142:         email: customerEmail,
 143:         first_name: customerName.split(" ")[0] ?? customerName,
 144:         last_name: customerName.split(" ").slice(1).join(" ") || "-",
 145:       },
 146:     };
 147: 
 148:     const { statusCode, body: payment } = await mpRequest({
 149:       method: "POST",
 150:       path: "/v1/payments",
 151:       body: paymentBody,
 152:       token,
 153:     });
 154: 
 155:     if (statusCode !== 201 || !payment.id) {
 156:       console.error("Erro MP:", statusCode, JSON.stringify(payment));
 157:       throw new HttpsError(
 158:         "internal",
 159:         payment?.message ?? "Erro ao criar pagamento no Mercado Pago."
 160:       );
 161:     }
 162: 
 163:     const pixCode =
 164:       payment.point_of_interaction?.transaction_data?.qr_code ?? "";
 165:     const pixQrCodeBase64 =
 166:       payment.point_of_interaction?.transaction_data?.qr_code_base64 ?? "";
 167:     const paymentId = String(payment.id);
 168: 
 169:     // 5. Salva dados do Pix no pedido
 170:     await orderRef.update({
 171:       pixCode,
 172:       pixQrCodeBase64,
 173:       paymentId,
 174:       mpStatus: payment.status,
 175:       sandbox: config.sandbox ?? true,
 176:       updatedAt: FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
 177:     });
 178: 
 179:     console.log(`Pix criado — orderId: ${orderId} | paymentId: ${paymentId} | sandbox: ${config.sandbox}`);
 180: 
 181:     return { pixCode, pixQrCodeBase64, paymentId };
 182:   }
 183: );
 184: 
 185: // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 186: // webhookMercadoPago
 187: // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 188: 
 189: exports.webhookMercadoPago = onRequest(
 190:   {
 191:     secrets: [mpAccessToken],
 192:   },
 193:   async (req, res) => {
 194:     // O MP exige resposta 200 imediata para não reenviar
 195:     res.status(200).send("OK");
 196: 
 197:     try {
 198:       // Aceita tanto query param (IPN legado) quanto body JSON (Webhooks v2)
 199:       const type = req.body?.type ?? req.query?.topic;
 200:       const dataId = req.body?.data?.id ?? req.query?.id;
 201: 
 202:       if (type !== "payment" || !dataId) {
 203:         console.log("Webhook ignorado — tipo:", type, "id:", dataId);
 204:         return;
 205:       }
 206: 
 207:       const token = mpAccessToken.value();
 208:       if (!token) {
 209:         console.error("Secret MERCADOPAGO_ACCESS_TOKEN não configurado.");
 210:         return;
 211:       }
 212: 
 213:       // Consulta o pagamento na API do MP para obter status atualizado
 214:       const { statusCode, body: payment } = await mpRequest({
 215:         method: "GET",
 216:         path: `/v1/payments/${dataId}`,
 217:         token,
 218:       });
 219: 
 220:       if (statusCode !== 200) {
 221:         console.error("Erro ao consultar pagamento:", statusCode, JSON.stringify(payment));
 222:         return;
 223:       }
 224: 
 225:       const orderId = payment.external_reference;
 226:       const mpStatus = payment.status; // approved | pending | rejected | cancelled
 227: 
 228:       if (!orderId) {
 229:         console.log("Webhook sem external_reference — paymentId:", dataId);
 230:         return;
 231:       }
 232: 
 233:       // Mapeia status MP → status do pedido
 234:       const statusMap = {
 235:         approved: "confirmed",
 236:         pending: "awaiting_payment",
 237:         in_process: "awaiting_payment",
 238:         rejected: "cancelled",
 239:         cancelled: "cancelled",
 240:         refunded: "cancelled",
 241:         charged_back: "cancelled",
 242:       };
 243: 
 244:       const orderStatus = statusMap[mpStatus] ?? "awaiting_payment";
 245: 
 246:       const db = getFirestore();
 247:       const orderRef = db.collection("orders").doc(orderId);
 248:       const orderSnap = await orderRef.get();
 249: 
 250:       if (!orderSnap.exists) {
 251:         console.error("Pedido não encontrado para orderId:", orderId);
 252:         return;
 253:       }
 254: 
 255:       await orderRef.update({
 256:         status: orderStatus,
 257:         mpStatus,
 258:         paymentId: String(payment.id),
 259:         updatedAt: FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
 260:       });
 261: 
 262:       console.log(`Webhook processado — orderId: ${orderId} | mpStatus: ${mpStatus} | orderStatus: ${orderStatus}`);
 263:     } catch (err) {
 264:       // Não relança — o 200 já foi enviado e o MP não vai reenviar
 265:       console.error("Erro no webhook:", err);
 266:     }
 267:   }
 268: );

==================================================
   1: //import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
   2: extension CurrencyFormat on double {
   3:   /// Formata como moeda brasileira: R$ 1.234,56
   4:   String toBRL() => 'R\$ ${toStringAsFixed(2).replaceAll(".", ",")}';
   5: }
   6: extension DateTimeDisplay on DateTime {
   7:   /// Ex.: 31/12/2025
   8:   String toDisplayDate() {
   9:     final d = day.toString().padLeft(2, '0');
  10:     final m = month.toString().padLeft(2, '0');
  11:     return '$d/$m/$year';
  12:   }
  13:   /// Ex.: 31/12/2025 23:59
  14:   String toDisplayDateTime() {
  15:     final h = hour.toString().padLeft(2, '0');
  16:     final min = minute.toString().padLeft(2, '0');
  17:     return '${toDisplayDate()} $h:$min';
  18:   }
  19: }

   1: import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
   2: import '../../data/models/order_model.dart';
   3: import '../constants/app_colors.dart';
   4: extension OrderStatusUiExtension on OrderStatus {
   5:   Color get color {
   6:     switch (this) {
   7:       case OrderStatus.awaitingPayment:
   8:         return AppColors.warning;
   9:       case OrderStatus.pending:
  10:         return AppColors.warning;
  11:       case OrderStatus.confirmed:
  12:         return AppColors.info;
  13:       case OrderStatus.shipped:
  14:         return AppColors.pink;
  15:       case OrderStatus.delivered:
  16:         return AppColors.success;
  17:       case OrderStatus.cancelled:
  18:         return AppColors.error;
  19:     }
  20:   }
  21:   IconData get icon {
  22:     switch (this) {
  23:       case OrderStatus.awaitingPayment:
  24:         return Icons.payments_outlined;
  25:       case OrderStatus.pending:
  26:         return Icons.hourglass_empty;
  27:       case OrderStatus.confirmed:
  28:         return Icons.check;
  29:       case OrderStatus.shipped:
  30:         return Icons.local_shipping_outlined;
  31:       case OrderStatus.delivered:
  32:         return Icons.done_all;
  33:       case OrderStatus.cancelled:
  34:         return Icons.cancel_outlined;
  35:     }
  36:   }
  37: }

   1: import 'package:cloud_firestore/cloud_firestore.dart';
   2: class OrderItemModel {
   3:   const OrderItemModel({
   4:     required this.productId,
   5:     required this.productName,
   6:     required this.productImageUrl,
   7:     required this.quantity,
   8:     required this.unitPrice,
   9:   });
  10:   final String productId;
  11:   final String productName;
  12:   final String productImageUrl;
  13:   final int quantity;
  14:   final double unitPrice;
  15:   double get subtotal => unitPrice * quantity;
  16:   Map<String, dynamic> toMap() {
  17:     return {
  18:       'productId': productId,
  19:       'productName': productName,
  20:       'productImageUrl': productImageUrl,
  21:       'quantity': quantity,
  22:       'unitPrice': unitPrice,
  23:     };
  24:   }
  25:   factory OrderItemModel.fromMap(Map<String, dynamic> map) {
  26:     return OrderItemModel(
  27:       productId: (map['productId'] ?? '').toString(),
  28:       productName: (map['productName'] ?? '').toString(),
  29:       productImageUrl: (map['productImageUrl'] ?? '').toString(),
  30:       quantity: (map['quantity'] as num?)?.toInt() ?? 1,
  31:       unitPrice: _parseDouble(map['unitPrice']),
  32:     );
  33:   }
  34:   static double _parseDouble(dynamic value) {
  35:     if (value is int) return value.toDouble();
  36:     if (value is double) return value;
  37:     if (value is String) return double.tryParse(value.replaceAll(',', '.')) ?? 0;
  38:     return 0;
  39:   }
  40: }
  41: enum OrderStatus {
  42:   awaitingPayment('awaiting_payment', 'Aguardando pagamento'),
  43:   pending('pending', 'Pendente'),
  44:   confirmed('confirmed', 'Confirmado'),
  45:   shipped('shipped', 'Enviado'),
  46:   delivered('delivered', 'Entregue'),
  47:   cancelled('cancelled', 'Cancelado');
  48:   const OrderStatus(this.value, this.label);
  49:   final String value;
  50:   final String label;
  51:   static OrderStatus fromValue(String value) {
  52:     return OrderStatus.values.firstWhere(
  53:       (s) => s.value == value,
  54:       orElse: () => OrderStatus.pending,
  55:     );
  56:   }
  57: }
  58: class OrderModel {
  59:   const OrderModel({
  60:     required this.id,
  61:     required this.customerId,
  62:     required this.customerName,
  63:     required this.customerEmail,
  64:     required this.items,
  65:     required this.total,
  66:     required this.status,
  67:     this.pixCode,
  68:     this.pixQrCodeBase64,
  69:     this.paymentId,
  70:     this.createdAt,
  71:     this.updatedAt,
  72:   });
  73:   final String id;
  74:   final String customerId;
  75:   final String customerName;
  76:   final String customerEmail;
  77:   final List<OrderItemModel> items;
  78:   final double total;
  79:   final String status;
  80:   // Dados do pagamento Pix
  81:   final String? pixCode;
  82:   final String? pixQrCodeBase64;
  83:   final String? paymentId;
  84:   final Timestamp? createdAt;
  85:   final Timestamp? updatedAt;
  86:   OrderStatus get orderStatus => OrderStatus.fromValue(status);
  87:   int get totalItems => items.fold(0, (acc, item) => acc + item.quantity);
  88:   bool get isPaid =>
  89:       orderStatus != OrderStatus.awaitingPayment &&
  90:       orderStatus != OrderStatus.cancelled;
  91:   Map<String, dynamic> toMap() {
  92:     return {
  93:       'customerId': customerId,
  94:       'customerName': customerName,
  95:       'customerEmail': customerEmail,
  96:       'items': items.map((i) => i.toMap()).toList(),
  97:       'total': total,
  98:       'status': status,
  99:       'pixCode': pixCode,
 100:       'pixQrCodeBase64': pixQrCodeBase64,
 101:       'paymentId': paymentId,
 102:       'createdAt': createdAt,
 103:       'updatedAt': updatedAt,
 104:     };
 105:   }
 106:   factory OrderModel.fromMap(String id, Map<String, dynamic> map) {
 107:     final rawItems = map['items'] as List<dynamic>? ?? [];
 108:     return OrderModel(
 109:       id: id,
 110:       customerId: (map['customerId'] ?? '').toString(),
 111:       customerName: (map['customerName'] ?? '').toString(),
 112:       customerEmail: (map['customerEmail'] ?? '').toString(),
 113:       items: rawItems
 114:           .map((i) => OrderItemModel.fromMap(i as Map<String, dynamic>))
 115:           .toList(),
 116:       total: _parseDouble(map['total']),
 117:       status: (map['status'] ?? 'awaiting_payment').toString(),
 118:       pixCode: map['pixCode'] as String?,
 119:       pixQrCodeBase64: map['pixQrCodeBase64'] as String?,
 120:       paymentId: map['paymentId'] as String?,
 121:       createdAt: map['createdAt'] as Timestamp?,
 122:       updatedAt: map['updatedAt'] as Timestamp?,
 123:     );
 124:   }
 125:   static double _parseDouble(dynamic value) {
 126:     if (value is int) return value.toDouble();
 127:     if (value is double) return value;
 128:     if (value is String) return double.tryParse(value.replaceAll(',', '.')) ?? 0;
 129:     return 0;
 130:   }
 131: }

   1: import 'package:cloud_firestore/cloud_firestore.dart';
   2: class ProductModel {
   3:   final String id;
   4:   final String name;
   5:   final String description;
   6:   final double price;
   7:   final String imageUrl;
   8:   final String category;
   9:   final bool isActive;
  10:   final bool isFeatured;
  11:   final Timestamp? createdAt;
  12:   final Timestamp? updatedAt;
  13:   const ProductModel({
  14:     required this.id,
  15:     required this.name,
  16:     required this.description,
  17:     required this.price,
  18:     required this.imageUrl,
  19:     required this.category,
  20:     required this.isActive,
  21:     required this.isFeatured,
  22:     required this.createdAt,
  23:     required this.updatedAt,
  24:   });
  25:   factory ProductModel.empty() {
  26:     return const ProductModel(
  27:       id: '',
  28:       name: '',
  29:       description: '',
  30:       price: 0,
  31:       imageUrl: '',
  32:       category: '',
  33:       isActive: true,
  34:       isFeatured: false,
  35:       createdAt: null,
  36:       updatedAt: null,
  37:     );
  38:   }
  39:   ProductModel copyWith({
  40:     String? id,
  41:     String? name,
  42:     String? description,
  43:     double? price,
  44:     String? imageUrl,
  45:     String? category,
  46:     bool? isActive,
  47:     bool? isFeatured,
  48:     Timestamp? createdAt,
  49:     Timestamp? updatedAt,
  50:   }) {
  51:     return ProductModel(
  52:       id: id ?? this.id,
  53:       name: name ?? this.name,
  54:       description: description ?? this.description,
  55:       price: price ?? this.price,
  56:       imageUrl: imageUrl ?? this.imageUrl,
  57:       category: category ?? this.category,
  58:       isActive: isActive ?? this.isActive,
  59:       isFeatured: isFeatured ?? this.isFeatured,
  60:       createdAt: createdAt ?? this.createdAt,
  61:       updatedAt: updatedAt ?? this.updatedAt,
  62:     );
  63:   }
  64:   Map<String, dynamic> toMap() {
  65:     return {
  66:       'name': name,
  67:       'description': description,
  68:       'price': price,
  69:       'imageUrl': imageUrl,
  70:       'category': category,
  71:       'isActive': isActive,
  72:       'isFeatured': isFeatured,
  73:       'createdAt': createdAt,
  74:       'updatedAt': updatedAt,
  75:     };
  76:   }
  77:   factory ProductModel.fromMap(String id, Map<String, dynamic> map) {
  78:     return ProductModel(
  79:       id: id,
  80:       name: (map['name'] ?? '').toString(),
  81:       description: (map['description'] ?? '').toString(),
  82:       price: _parsePrice(map['price']),
  83:       imageUrl: (map['imageUrl'] ?? '').toString(),
  84:       category: (map['category'] ?? '').toString(),
  85:       isActive: map['isActive'] == true,
  86:       isFeatured: map['isFeatured'] == true,
  87:       createdAt: map['createdAt'] as Timestamp?,
  88:       updatedAt: map['updatedAt'] as Timestamp?,
  89:     );
  90:   }
  91:   static double _parsePrice(dynamic value) {
  92:     if (value is int) {
  93:       return value.toDouble();
  94:     }
  95:     if (value is double) {
  96:       return value;
  97:     }
  98:     if (value is String) {
  99:       return double.tryParse(value.replaceAll(',', '.')) ?? 0;
 100:     }
 101:     return 0;

   1: import 'package:cloud_firestore/cloud_firestore.dart';
   2: import '../models/order_model.dart';
   3: class OrderRepository {
   4:   OrderRepository({FirebaseFirestore? firestore})
   5:       : _db = firestore ?? FirebaseFirestore.instance;
   6:   final FirebaseFirestore _db;
   7:   CollectionReference<Map<String, dynamic>> get _ordersRef =>
   8:       _db.collection('orders');
   9:   Future<String> createOrder(OrderModel order) async {
  10:     final now = FieldValue.serverTimestamp();
  11:     final doc = await _ordersRef.add({
  12:       ...order.toMap(),
  13:       'createdAt': now,
  14:       'updatedAt': now,
  15:     });
  16:     return doc.id;
  17:   }
  18:   Future<void> updatePaymentData({
  19:     required String orderId,
  20:     required String pixCode,
  21:     required String pixQrCodeBase64,
  22:     required String paymentId,
  23:   }) async {
  24:     await _ordersRef.doc(orderId).update({
  25:       'pixCode': pixCode,
  26:       'pixQrCodeBase64': pixQrCodeBase64,
  27:       'paymentId': paymentId,
  28:       'updatedAt': FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
  29:     });
  30:   }
  31:   Stream<OrderModel?> watchOrder(String orderId) {
  32:     return _ordersRef.doc(orderId).snapshots().map((snap) {
  33:       if (!snap.exists || snap.data() == null) return null;
  34:       return OrderModel.fromMap(snap.id, snap.data()!);
  35:     });
  36:   }
  37:   Stream<List<OrderModel>> watchCustomerOrders(String customerId) {
  38:     return _ordersRef
  39:         .where('customerId', isEqualTo: customerId)
  40:         .orderBy('createdAt', descending: true)
  41:         .snapshots()
  42:         .map(_mapCollection);
  43:   }
  44:   Stream<List<OrderModel>> watchAllOrders() {
  45:     return _ordersRef
  46:         .orderBy('createdAt', descending: true)
  47:         .snapshots()
  48:         .map(_mapCollection);
  49:   }
  50:   Stream<List<OrderModel>> watchOrdersByStatus(String status) {
  51:     return _ordersRef
  52:         .where('status', isEqualTo: status)
  53:         .orderBy('createdAt', descending: true)
  54:         .snapshots()
  55:         .map(_mapCollection);
  56:   }
  57:   Future<void> updateStatus(String orderId, String status) async {
  58:     await _ordersRef.doc(orderId).update({
  59:       'status': status,
  60:       'updatedAt': FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
  61:     });
  62:   }
  63:   List<OrderModel> _mapCollection(
  64:     QuerySnapshot<Map<String, dynamic>> snapshot,
  65:   ) {
  66:     return snapshot.docs
  67:         .map((doc) => OrderModel.fromMap(doc.id, doc.data()))
  68:         .toList();
  69:   }
  70: }

   1: import 'package:cloud_firestore/cloud_firestore.dart';
   2: import '../models/product_model.dart';
   3: class ProductPage {
   4:   const ProductPage({required this.products, this.lastDoc});
   5:   final List<ProductModel> products;
   6:   final DocumentSnapshot? lastDoc;
   7: }
   8: class ProductRepository {
   9:   ProductRepository({
  10:     FirebaseFirestore? firestore,
  11:   }) : _firestore = firestore ?? FirebaseFirestore.instance;
  12:   final FirebaseFirestore _firestore;
  13:   CollectionReference<Map<String, dynamic>> get _productsRef =>
  14:       _firestore.collection('products');
  15:   Stream<List<ProductModel>> watchActiveProducts() {
  16:     return _productsRef
  17:         .where('isActive', isEqualTo: true)
  18:         .orderBy('name')
  19:         .snapshots()
  20:         .map(_mapCollection);
  21:   }
  22:   Stream<List<ProductModel>> watchAllProducts() {
  23:     return _productsRef.orderBy('name').snapshots().map(_mapCollection);
  24:   }
  25:   Stream<List<ProductModel>> watchFeaturedProducts() {
  26:     return _productsRef
  27:         .where('isActive', isEqualTo: true)
  28:         .where('isFeatured', isEqualTo: true)
  29:         .orderBy('name')
  30:         .snapshots()
  31:         .map(_mapCollection);
  32:   }
  33:   /// Busca uma página de produtos ativos. [startAfter] é o último documento
  34:   /// da página anterior (null = primeira página).
  35:   Future<ProductPage> getActiveProductsPage({
  36:     required int limit,
  37:     DocumentSnapshot? startAfter,
  38:   }) async {
  39:     var query = _productsRef
  40:         .where('isActive', isEqualTo: true)
  41:         .orderBy('name')
  42:         .limit(limit);
  43:     if (startAfter != null) {
  44:       query = query.startAfterDocument(startAfter);
  45:     }
  46:     final snapshot = await query.get();
  47:     final docs = snapshot.docs;
  48:     return ProductPage(
  49:       products: docs
  50:           .map((doc) => ProductModel.fromMap(doc.id, doc.data()))
  51:           .toList(),
  52:       lastDoc: docs.isNotEmpty ? docs.last : null,
  53:     );
  54:   }
  55:   Future<ProductModel?> getProductById(String productId) async {
  56:     final snapshot = await _productsRef.doc(productId).get();
  57:     if (!snapshot.exists || snapshot.data() == null) {
  58:       return null;
  59:     }
  60:     return ProductModel.fromMap(snapshot.id, snapshot.data()!);
  61:   }
  62:   Future<String> createProduct(ProductModel product) async {
  63:     final now = FieldValue.serverTimestamp();
  64:     final doc = await _productsRef.add({
  65:       ...product.toMap(),
  66:       'createdAt': now,
  67:       'updatedAt': now,
  68:     });
  69:     return doc.id;
  70:   }
  71:   Future<void> updateProduct(ProductModel product) async {
  72:     await _productsRef.doc(product.id).update({
  73:       ...product.toMap(),
  74:       'updatedAt': FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
  75:     });
  76:   }
  77:   Future<void> setProductActive({
  78:     required String productId,
  79:     required bool isActive,
  80:   }) async {
  81:     await _productsRef.doc(productId).update({
  82:       'isActive': isActive,
  83:       'updatedAt': FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
  84:     });
  85:   }
  86:   Future<void> deleteProduct(String productId) async {

  44:   Future<int> getUsersCount() async {
  45:     final snapshot = await _usersRef.count().get();
  46:     return snapshot.count ?? 0;
  47:   }
  48:   Future<int> getMasterCount() async {
  49:     final snapshot = await _usersRef.where('role', isEqualTo: 'master').count().get();
  50:     return snapshot.count ?? 0;
  51:   }
  52:   Future<bool> isLastMaster(String uid) async {
  53:     final user = await getUser(uid);
  54:     if (user == null || !user.isMaster) {
  55:       return false;
  56:     }
  57:     final masterCount = await getMasterCount();
  58:     return masterCount <= 1;
  59:   }
  60: }

ARQUIVO: C:\Users\Alex Salles\Apps - desenvolvimento\petjoy_app\lib\data\services\xlsx_import_service.dart
==================================================
   1: import 'dart:io';
   2: import 'package:cloud_firestore/cloud_firestore.dart';
   3: import 'package:excel/excel.dart';
   4: class XlsxImportResult {
   5:   const XlsxImportResult({
   6:     required this.criados,
   7:     required this.atualizados,
   8:     required this.erros,
   9:     required this.mensagensErro,
  10:   });
  11:   final int criados;
  12:   final int atualizados;
  13:   final int erros;
  14:   final List<String> mensagensErro;
  15:   bool get sucesso => erros == 0;
  16:   int get total => criados + atualizados;
  17: }
  18: class _ProdutoXlsx {
  19:   const _ProdutoXlsx({
  20:     required this.nome,
  21:     required this.quantidade,
  22:     required this.preco,
  23:     required this.animal,
  24:   });
  25:   final String nome;
  26:   final String quantidade;
  27:   final double preco;
  28:   final String animal;
  29: }
  30: class XlsxImportService {
  31:   XlsxImportService({FirebaseFirestore? firestore})
  32:       : _db = firestore ?? FirebaseFirestore.instance;
  33:   final FirebaseFirestore _db;
  34:   /// Lê o arquivo .xlsx e importa os produtos para o Firestore.
  35:   ///
  36:   /// Formato esperado da planilha:
  37:   ///   Linha 1: cabeçalho (Nome | Quantity | Preço | Animal)
  38:   ///   Linha 2+: dados
  39:   ///   Coluna A: Nome
  40:   ///   Coluna B: Quantity (ex: 250g)
  41:   ///   Coluna C: Preço (número)
  42:   ///   Coluna D: Animal (cachorro | gato | ambos)
  43:   Future<XlsxImportResult> importar(File arquivo) async {
  44:     final bytes = await arquivo.readAsBytes();
  45:     final workbook = Excel.decodeBytes(bytes);
  46:     final sheetName = workbook.sheets.keys.first;
  47:     final sheet = workbook.sheets[sheetName]!;
  48:     final produtos = _lerProdutos(sheet);
  49:     if (produtos.isEmpty) {
  50:       return const XlsxImportResult(
  51:         criados: 0,
  52:         atualizados: 0,
  53:         erros: 1,
  54:         mensagensErro: ['Nenhum produto encontrado na planilha.'],
  55:       );
  56:     }
  57:     return _salvarNoBanco(produtos);
  58:   }
  59:   List<_ProdutoXlsx> _lerProdutos(Sheet sheet) {
  60:     final produtos = <_ProdutoXlsx>[];
  61:     // Linha 0 = cabeçalho, começa na linha 1
  62:     for (int i = 1; i < sheet.maxRows; i++) {
  63:       final row = sheet.row(i);
  64:       final nome = _cellString(row, 0);
  65:       final quantidade = _cellString(row, 1);
  66:       final precoRaw = _cellString(row, 2);
  67:       final animal = _cellString(row, 3).toLowerCase();
  68:       if (nome.isEmpty) continue;
  69:       final preco = double.tryParse(
  70:             precoRaw
  71:                 .replaceAll('R\$', '')
  72:                 .replaceAll('.', '')
  73:                 .replaceAll(',', '.')
  74:                 .trim(),
  75:           ) ??
  76:           0;
  77:       if (preco <= 0) continue;
  78:       produtos.add(_ProdutoXlsx(
  79:         nome: nome,
  80:         quantidade: quantidade,
  81:         preco: preco,
  82:         animal: animal,
  83:       ));
  84:     }
  85:     return produtos;
  86:   }
  87:   String _cellString(List<Data?> row, int index) {
  88:     if (index >= row.length) return '';
  89:     final cell = row[index];
  90:     if (cell == null || cell.value == null) return '';
  91:     return cell.value.toString().trim();
  92:   }
  93:   String _mapCategoria(String animal) {
  94:     switch (animal) {
  95:       case 'cachorro':
  96:         return 'Cachorro';
  97:       case 'gato':
  98:         return 'Gato';
  99:       case 'ambos':
 100:         return 'Ambos';
 101:       default:
 102:         return animal.isNotEmpty ? animal : 'Geral';
 103:     }
 104:   }
 105:   Future<XlsxImportResult> _salvarNoBanco(List<_ProdutoXlsx> produtos) async {
 106:     final colecao = _db.collection('products');
 107:     int criados = 0;
 108:     int atualizados = 0;
 109:     int erros = 0;
 110:     final mensagensErro = <String>[];
 111:     for (final p in produtos) {
 112:       try {
 113:         final descricao = p.quantidade.isNotEmpty ? 'Embalagem: ${p.quantidade}' : '';
 114:         final categoria = _mapCategoria(p.animal);
 115:         final agora = FieldValue.serverTimestamp();
 116:         final snapshot = await colecao
 117:             .where('name', isEqualTo: p.nome)
 118:             .where('description', isEqualTo: descricao)
 119:             .limit(1)
 120:             .get();
 121:         if (snapshot.docs.isNotEmpty) {
 122:           await snapshot.docs.first.reference.update({
 123:             'price': p.preco,
 124:             'category': categoria,
 125:             'updatedAt': agora,
 126:           });
 127:           atualizados++;
 128:         } else {
 129:           await colecao.add({
 130:             'name': p.nome,
 131:             'description': descricao,
 132:             'price': p.preco,
 133:             'category': categoria,
 134:             'imageUrl': '',
 135:             'isActive': true,
 136:             'isFeatured': false,
 137:             'createdAt': agora,
 138:             'updatedAt': agora,
 139:           });
 140:           criados++;
 141:         }
 142:       } catch (e) {
 143:         erros++;
 144:         mensagensErro.add('${p.nome}: ${e.toString()}');
 145:       }
 146:     }
 147:     return XlsxImportResult(
 148:       criados: criados,
 149:       atualizados: atualizados,
 150:       erros: erros,
 151:       mensagensErro: mensagensErro,
 152:     );
 153:   }
 154: }

  31:       email: email.trim(),

  33:     );

  35:   }
  36:   Future<void> registerWithEmail({
  37:     required String name,
  38:     required String email,
  39:     required String password,
  40:   }) async {
  41:     // 1. Cria a conta no Firebase Auth PRIMEIRO (agora o usuário está autenticado)
  42:     final credential = await _auth.createUserWithEmailAndPassword(
  43:       email: email.trim(),
  44:       password: password,
  45:     );
  46:     final user = credential.user;
  47:     if (user == null) {
  48:       throw FirebaseAuthException(
  49:         code: 'user-not-created',
  50:         message: 'Não foi possível criar o usuário.',
  51:       );
  52:     }
  53:     await user.updateDisplayName(name.trim());
  54:     // 2. Agora autenticado, consulta o Firestore com segurança
  55:     final usersCount = await _userRepository.getUsersCount();
  56:     final role = usersCount == 0 ? 'master' : 'user';
  57:     // 3. Salva o documento do usuário
  58:     await _userRepository.createUser(
  59:       UserModel(
  60:         uid: user.uid,
  61:         name: name.trim(),
  62:         email: email.trim(),
  63:         role: role,
  64:       ),
  65:     );
  66:   }
  67:   Future<void> sendPasswordResetEmail(String email) async {
  68:     await _auth.sendPasswordResetEmail(email: email.trim());
  69:   }
  70:   Future<void> signOut() async {
  71:     await _auth.signOut();
  72:   }
  73:   Future<void> _ensureUserDocument(User? user) async {
  74:     if (user == null) {
  75:       return;
  76:     }
  77:     final existingUser = await _userRepository.getUser(user.uid);
  78:     if (existingUser != null) {
  79:       return;
  80:     }
  81:     final usersCount = await _userRepository.getUsersCount();
  82:     final role = usersCount == 0 ? 'master' : 'user';
  83:     await _userRepository.createUser(
  84:       UserModel(
  85:         uid: user.uid,
  86:         name: user.displayName?.trim().isNotEmpty == true
  87:             ? user.displayName!.trim()
  88:             : user.email?.split('@').first ?? 'Usuário',
  89:         email: user.email ?? '',
  90:         role: role,
  91:       ),
  92:     );
  93:   }
  94: }

   1: import 'package:flutter_riverpod/flutter_riverpod.dart';
   2: import '../../../data/models/cart_item_model.dart';
   3: import '../../../data/models/product_model.dart';
   4: 
   5: class CartState {
   6:   const CartState({this.items = const []});
   7:   final List<CartItemModel> items;
   8:   int get totalItems => items.fold(0, (acc, item) => acc + item.quantity);
   9:   double get totalPrice => items.fold(0.0, (acc, item) => acc + item.subtotal);
  10:   bool containsProduct(String productId) =>
  11:       items.any((item) => item.product.id == productId);
  12:   int quantityOf(String productId) {
  13:     final index = items.indexWhere((i) => i.product.id == productId);
  14:     return index >= 0 ? items[index].quantity : 0;
  15:   }
  16: 
  17:   CartState copyWith({List<CartItemModel>? items}) {
  18:     return CartState(items: items ?? this.items);
  19:   }
  20: }
  21: 
  22: class CartNotifier extends StateNotifier<CartState> {
  23:   CartNotifier() : super(const CartState());
  24:   void add(ProductModel product) {
  25:     final index = state.items.indexWhere((i) => i.product.id == product.id);
  26:     if (index >= 0) {
  27:       final updated = List<CartItemModel>.from(state.items);
  28:       updated[index] = updated[index].copyWith(
  29:         quantity: updated[index].quantity + 1,
  30:       );
  31:       state = state.copyWith(items: updated);
  32:     } else {
  33:       state = state.copyWith(
  34:         items: [
  35:           ...state.items,
  36:           CartItemModel(product: product, quantity: 1),
  37:         ],
  38:       );
  39:     }
  40:   }
  41: 
  42:   void remove(String productId) {
  43:     state = state.copyWith(
  44:       items: state.items.where((i) => i.product.id != productId).toList(),
  45:     );
  46:   }
  47: 
  48:   void increment(String productId) {
  49:     final updated = state.items.map((item) {
  50:       if (item.product.id == productId) {
  51:         return item.copyWith(quantity: item.quantity + 1);
  52:       }
  53:       return item;
  54:     }).toList();
  55:     state = state.copyWith(items: updated);
  56:   }
  57: 
  58:   void decrement(String productId) {
  59:     final index = state.items.indexWhere((i) => i.product.id == productId);
  60:     if (index < 0) return;
  61:     if (state.items[index].quantity <= 1) {
  62:       remove(productId);
  63:       return;
  64:     }
  65:     final updated = state.items.map((item) {
  66:       if (item.product.id == productId) {
  67:         return item.copyWith(quantity: item.quantity - 1);
  68:       }
  69:       return item;
  70:     }).toList();
  71:     state = state.copyWith(items: updated);
  72:   }
  73: 
  74:   void clear() {
  75:     state = const CartState();
  76:   }
  77: }
  78: 
  79: final cartProvider = StateNotifierProvider<CartNotifier, CartState>((ref) {
  80:   return CartNotifier();
  81: });

  79:   /// Cria o pedido no Firestore e gera o Pix via Cloud Function.
  80:   /// Retorna [PixPaymentData] com QR Code e código copia-e-cola.
  81:   Future<PixPaymentData> placeOrderWithPix({
  82:     required String customerId,
  83:     required String customerName,
  84:     required String customerEmail,
  85:     required List<CartItemModel> items,
  86:   }) async {
  87:     // 1. Verifica se MP está configurado
  88:     final config = await _configRepository.getConfig();
  89:     if (!config.isConfigured) {
  90:       throw Exception(
  91:         'Pagamento não configurado. Solicite ao administrador que configure o Mercado Pago.',
  92:       );
  93:     }
  94:     // 2. Monta itens do pedido
  95:     final orderItems = items
  96:         .map(
  97:           (i) => OrderItemModel(
  98:             productId: i.product.id,
  99:             productName: i.product.name,
 100:             productImageUrl: i.product.imageUrl,
 101:             quantity: i.quantity,
 102:             unitPrice: i.product.price,
 103:           ),
 104:         )
 105:         .toList();

 107:     // 3. Cria pedido com status awaiting_payment
 108:     final order = OrderModel(
 109:       id: '',
 110:       customerId: customerId,
 111:       customerName: customerName,
 112:       customerEmail: customerEmail,
 113:       items: orderItems,
 114:       total: total,
 115:       status: OrderStatus.awaitingPayment.value,
 116:     );
 117:     final orderId = await _repository.createOrder(order);
 118:     // 4. Chama Cloud Function para gerar Pix
 119:     final functions = FirebaseFunctions.instanceFor(
 120:       region: 'southamerica-east1',
 121:     );
 122:     final callable = functions.httpsCallable('criarPagamentoPix');
 123:     final result = await callable.call({
 124:       'orderId': orderId,
 125:       'total': total,
 126:       'customerEmail': customerEmail,
 127:       'customerName': customerName,
 128:     });
 129:     final data = Map<String, dynamic>.from(result.data as Map);
 130:     final pixCode = data['pixCode'] as String;
 131:     final pixQrCodeBase64 = data['pixQrCodeBase64'] as String;
 132:     final paymentId = data['paymentId'].toString();
 133:     // 5. Salva dados do Pix no pedido
 134:     //await _repository.updatePaymentData(
 135:     //orderId: orderId,
 136:     //pixCode: pixCode,
 137:     //pixQrCodeBase64: pixQrCodeBase64,
 138:     //paymentId: paymentId,
 139:     //);
 140:     return PixPaymentData(
 141:       orderId: orderId,
 142:       pixCode: pixCode,
 143:       pixQrCodeBase64: pixQrCodeBase64,
 144:       paymentId: paymentId,
 145:     );
 146:   }

  56:   final ProductRepository _repository;
  57:   Future<void> fetchFirst() async {

  64:         products: page.products,
  65:         lastDoc: page.lastDoc,
  66:         hasMore: page.products.length >= _kPageSize,
  67:         isLoading: false,
  68:       );
  69:     } catch (e) {
  70:       state = ProductPageState(isLoading: false, error: e.toString());
  71:     }
  72:   }
  73:   Future<void> loadMore() async {
  74:     if (state.isLoading || !state.hasMore || state.lastDoc == null) return;
  75:     state = state.copyWith(isLoading: true);
  76:     try {
  77:       final page = await _repository.getActiveProductsPage(
  78:         limit: _kPageSize,
  79:         startAfter: state.lastDoc,
  80:       );
  81:       state = state.copyWith(
  82:         products: [...state.products, ...page.products],
  83:         lastDoc: page.lastDoc,
  84:         hasMore: page.products.length >= _kPageSize,
  85:         isLoading: false,
  86:         clearError: true,
  87:       );
  88:     } catch (e) {
  89:       state = state.copyWith(isLoading: false, error: e.toString());
  90:     }
  91:   }
  92: }
  93: final productPaginationProvider =
  94:     StateNotifierProvider<ProductPaginationNotifier, ProductPageState>(
  95:   (ref) => ProductPaginationNotifier(ref.read(productRepositoryProvider)),
  96: );
  97: // ---- Ações de escrita (admin) ----
  98: final productActionsProvider = Provider<ProductActions>((ref) {
  99:   return ProductActions(
 100:     repository: ref.read(productRepositoryProvider),
 101:     imageUploadService: ref.read(imageUploadServiceProvider),
 102:   );
 103: });
 104: class ProductActions {
 105:   const ProductActions({
 106:     required ProductRepository repository,
 107:     required ImageUploadService imageUploadService,
 108:   })  : _repository = repository,
 109:         _imageUploadService = imageUploadService;
 110:   final ProductRepository _repository;
 111:   final ImageUploadService _imageUploadService;
 112:   Future<void> createProduct({
 113:     required String name,
 114:     required String description,
 115:     required double price,
 116:     required String category,
 117:     required bool isActive,
 118:     required bool isFeatured,
 119:     File? imageFile,
 120:   }) async {
 121:     var imageUrl = '';
 122:     if (imageFile != null) {
 123:       final fileName =
 124:           '${DateTime.now().millisecondsSinceEpoch}_${_sanitizeFileName(name)}.jpg';
 125:       imageUrl = await _imageUploadService.uploadProductImage(
 126:         file: imageFile,
 127:         fileName: fileName,
 128:       );
 129:     }
 130:     final product = ProductModel.empty().copyWith(
 131:       name: name.trim(),
 132:       description: description.trim(),
 133:       price: price,
 134:       category: category.trim(),
 135:       imageUrl: imageUrl,
 136:       isActive: isActive,
 137:       isFeatured: isFeatured,
 138:     );
 139:     await _repository.createProduct(product);
 140:   }
 141:   Future<void> updateProduct({
 142:     required ProductModel product,
 143:     File? newImageFile,
 144:   }) async {
 145:     var imageUrl = product.imageUrl;
 146:     if (newImageFile != null) {
 147:       final fileName =
 148:           '${DateTime.now().millisecondsSinceEpoch}_${_sanitizeFileName(product.name)}.jpg';
 149:       imageUrl = await _imageUploadService.uploadProductImage(
 150:         file: newImageFile,
 151:         fileName: fileName,
 152:       );
 153:     }
 154:     await _repository.updateProduct(product.copyWith(imageUrl: imageUrl));
 155:   }
 156:   Future<void> setProductActive({
 157:     required String productId,
 158:     required bool isActive,
 159:   }) async {
 160:     await _repository.setProductActive(
 161:       productId: productId,
 162:       isActive: isActive,
 163:     );
 164:   }
 165:   Future<void> deleteProduct(String productId) async {
 166:     await _repository.deleteProduct(productId);
 167:   }
 168:   String _sanitizeFileName(String value) {
 169:     final normalized = value
 170:         .toLowerCase()
 171:         .replaceAll(RegExp(r'[^a-z0-9]+'), '_')
 172:         .replaceAll(RegExp(r'_+'), '_')
 173:         .replaceAll(RegExp(r'^_|_$'), '');
 174:     return normalized.isEmpty ? 'produto' : normalized;
 175:   }
 176: }

   1: import 'package:flutter_riverpod/flutter_riverpod.dart';
   2: import '../../data/models/user_model.dart';
   3: import 'auth_provider.dart';
   4: 
   5: final currentUserProfileProvider = StreamProvider<UserModel?>((ref) {
   6:   final authState = ref.watch(authStateProvider);
   7:   return authState.when(
   8:     data: (user) {
   9:       if (user == null) {
  10:         return Stream.value(null);
  11:       }
  12:       return ref.read(userRepositoryProvider).watchUser(user.uid);
  13:     },
  14:     loading: () => Stream.value(null),
  15:     error: (_, _) => Stream.value(null),
  16:   );
  17: });
  18: // Stream de todos os usuários — usado pelo painel admin
  19: final allUsersProvider = StreamProvider<List<UserModel>>((ref) {
  20:   final currentUser = ref.watch(currentUserProfileProvider).value;
  21:   if (currentUser == null || !currentUser.isMaster) return Stream.value([]);
  22:   return ref.read(userRepositoryProvider).watchAllUsers();
  23: });

  12:   final _formKey = GlobalKey<FormState>();
  13:   final _nameController = TextEditingController();
  14:   final _emailController = TextEditingController();
  15:   final _passwordController = TextEditingController();
  16:   bool _isLogin = true;
  17:   bool _isLoading = false;
  18:   bool _passwordVisible = false;
  19:   @override
  20:   void dispose() {
  21:     _nameController.dispose();
  22:     _emailController.dispose();
  23:     _passwordController.dispose();
  24:     super.dispose();
  25:   }
  26:   Future<void> _submit() async {
  27:     if (!_formKey.currentState!.validate()) {
  28:       return;
  29:     }
  30:     FocusScope.of(context).unfocus();
  31:     setState(() {
  32:       _isLoading = true;
  33:     });
  34:     try {
  35:       final authService = ref.read(authServiceProvider);
  36:       if (_isLogin) {
  37:         await authService.signInWithEmail(
  38:           email: _emailController.text,
  39:           password: _passwordController.text.trim(),
  40:         );
  41:       } else {
  42:         await authService.registerWithEmail(
  43:           name: _nameController.text,
  44:           email: _emailController.text,
  45:           password: _passwordController.text.trim(),
  46:         );
  47:       }
  48:       if (!mounted) {
  49:         return;
  50:       }
  51:       Navigator.of(context).pushAndRemoveUntil(
  52:         MaterialPageRoute(builder: (_) => const HomeScreen()),
  53:         (route) => false,
  54:       );
  55:     } on FirebaseAuthException catch (error) {
  56:       if (!mounted) {
  57:         return;
  58:       }
  59:       ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
  60:         SnackBar(
  61:           content: Text(_mapAuthError(error)),
  62:         ),
  63:       );
  64:     } catch (_) {
  65:       if (!mounted) {
  66:         return;
  67:       }
  68:       ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
  69:         const SnackBar(
  70:           content: Text('Não foi possível concluir a operação.'),
  71:         ),
  72:       );
  73:     } finally {
  74:       if (mounted) {
  75:         setState(() {
  76:           _isLoading = false;
  77:         });
  78:       }
  79:     }
  80:   }
  81:   Future<void> _resetPassword() async {
  82:     final email = _emailController.text.trim();
  83:     if (email.isEmpty) {
  84:       ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
  85:         const SnackBar(
  86:           content: Text('Informe seu e-mail para recuperar a senha.'),
  87:         ),
  88:       );
  89:       return;
  90:     }
  91:     try {
  92:       await ref.read(authServiceProvider).sendPasswordResetEmail(email);
  93:       if (!mounted) {
  94:         return;
  95:       }
  96:       ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
  97:         const SnackBar(
  98:           content: Text('E-mail de recuperacao enviado.'),
  99:         ),
 100:       );
 101:     } on FirebaseAuthException catch (error) {
 102:       if (!mounted) {
 103:         return;
 104:       }
 105:       ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
 106:         SnackBar(
 107:           content: Text(_mapAuthError(error)),
 108:         ),
 109:       );
 110:     }
 111:   }
 112:   String _mapAuthError(FirebaseAuthException error) {
 113:     switch (error.code) {
 114:       case 'invalid-email':
 115:         return 'E-mail inválido.';
 116:       case 'email-already-in-use':
 117:         return 'Este e-mail ja esta em uso.';
 118:       case 'weak-password':
 119:         return 'A senha deve ter pelo menos 6 caracteres.';
 120:       case 'invalid-credential':
 121:       case 'wrong-password':
 122:       case 'user-not-found':
 123:         return 'E-mail ou senha inválidos.';
 124:       case 'too-many-requests':
 125:         return 'Muitas tentativas. Tente novamente mais tarde.';
 126:       default:
 127:         return error.message ?? 'Falha na autenticação.';
 128:     }
 129:   }

   1: import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

  10:   Widget build(BuildContext context, WidgetRef ref) {

  15: class _AdminImportScreenState extends ConsumerState<AdminImportScreen> {
  16:   final _service = XlsxImportService();
  17:   bool _isLoading = false;
  18:   String? _arquivoNome;
  19:   File? _arquivoSelecionado;
  20:   XlsxImportResult? _resultado;
  21:   Future<void> _selecionarArquivo() async {
  22:     final result = await FilePicker.platform.pickFiles(
  23:       type: FileType.custom,
  24:       allowedExtensions: ['xlsx'],
  25:     );
  26:     if (result == null || result.files.single.path == null) return;
  27:     setState(() {
  28:       _arquivoSelecionado = File(result.files.single.path!);
  29:       _arquivoNome = result.files.single.name;
  30:       _resultado = null;
  31:     });
  32:   }
  33: 
  34:   Future<void> _importar() async {
  35:     if (_arquivoSelecionado == null) return;
  36:     setState(() {
  37:       _isLoading = true;
  38:       _resultado = null;
  39:     });
  40:     try {
  41:       final resultado = await _service.importar(_arquivoSelecionado!);
  42:       setState(() => _resultado = resultado);
  43:     } catch (e) {
  44:       setState(() {
  45:         _resultado = XlsxImportResult(
  46:           criados: 0,
  47:           atualizados: 0,
  48:           erros: 1,
  49:           mensagensErro: [e.toString()],
  50:         );
  51:       });
  52:     } finally {
  53:       setState(() => _isLoading = false);
  54:     }
  55:   }
  56:

 225:   String _formatDateTime(DateTime date) => date.toDisplayDateTime();
 226:   @override
 227:   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
 228:     final date = order.createdAt?.toDate();
 229:     final dateStr = date != null ? _formatDateTime(date) : '—';
 230:     final shortId = '#${order.id.substring(0, 8).toUpperCase()}';
 231:     return DraggableScrollableSheet(
 232:       expand: false,
 233:       initialChildSize: 0.85,
 234:       maxChildSize: 0.95,

 236:         return Padding(

 354:   const _StatusButton({
 355:     required this.status,
 356:     required this.isSelected,
 357:     required this.onTap,
 358:   });

 360:   final bool isSelected;
 361:   final VoidCallback onTap;
 362:   @override
 363:   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
 364:     final color = status.color;
 365:     return GestureDetector(
 366:       onTap: isSelected ? null : onTap,

 368:         duration: const Duration(milliseconds: 200),
 369:         padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16, vertical: 10),
 370:         decoration: BoxDecoration(
 371:           color: isSelected ? color : color.withValues(alpha: 0.1),
 372:           borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(24),
 373:           border: Border.all(
 374:             color: color.withValues(alpha: isSelected ? 1.0 : 0.3),
 375:           ),
 376:         ),
 377:         child: Text(
 378:           status.label,
 379:           style: TextStyle(
 380:             fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
 381:             color: isSelected ? AppColors.white : color,
 382:             fontSize: 13,
 383:           ),
 384:         ),
 385:       ),
 386:     );
 387:   }
 388: }

ARQUIVO: C:\Users\Alex Salles\Apps - desenvolvimento\petjoy_app\lib\presentation\screens\admin\admin_products_screen.dart

   1: import 'dart:io';
   2: import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
   3: import 'package:flutter_riverpod/flutter_riverpod.dart';
   4: import 'package:image_picker/image_picker.dart';
   5: import '../../../core/constants/app_colors.dart';
   6: import '../../../data/models/product_model.dart';
   7: import '../../providers/product_provider.dart';
   8: import '../../../core/extensions/format_extensions.dart';
   9: import '../../providers/user_provider.dart';
  10: 
  11: class AdminProductsScreen extends ConsumerStatefulWidget {
  12:   const AdminProductsScreen({super.key});
  13:   @override
  14:   ConsumerState<AdminProductsScreen> createState() =>
  15:       _AdminProductsScreenState();
  16: }
  17: 
  18: class _AdminProductsScreenState extends ConsumerState<AdminProductsScreen> {
  19:   final _formKey = GlobalKey<FormState>();
  20:   final _nameController = TextEditingController();
  21:   final _descriptionController = TextEditingController();
  22:   final _priceController = TextEditingController();
  23:   final _categoryController = TextEditingController();
  24:   bool _isActive = true;
  25:   bool _isFeatured = false;
  26:   bool _isSaving = false;
  27:   File? _selectedImage;
  28:   // Quando não-nulo, estamos editando um produto existente
  29:   ProductModel? _editingProduct;
  30:   @override
  31:   void dispose() {
  32:     _nameController.dispose();
  33:     _descriptionController.dispose();
  34:     _priceController.dispose();
  35:     _categoryController.dispose();
  36:     super.dispose();
  37:   }
  38: 
  39:   void _startEditing(ProductModel product) {
  40:     setState(() {
  41:       _editingProduct = product;
  42:       _nameController.text = product.name;
  43:       _descriptionController.text = product.description;
  44:       _priceController.text = product.price
  45:           .toStringAsFixed(2)
  46:           .replaceAll('.', ',');
  47:       _categoryController.text = product.category;
  48:       _isActive = product.isActive;
  49:       _isFeatured = product.isFeatured;
  50:       _selectedImage = null;
  51:     });
  52:     Scrollable.ensureVisible(
  53:       _formKey.currentContext ?? context,
  54:       duration: const Duration(milliseconds: 300),
  55:       curve: Curves.easeOut,
  56:     );
  57:   }
  58: 
  59:   void _cancelEditing() {
  60:     setState(() {
  61:       _editingProduct = null;
  62:       _selectedImage = null;
  63:       _isActive = true;
  64:       _isFeatured = false;
  65:     });
  66:     _formKey.currentState?.reset();
  67:     _nameController.clear();
  68:     _descriptionController.clear();
  69:     _priceController.clear();
  70:     _categoryController.clear();
  71:   }
  72: 
  73:   Future<void> _pickImage() async {
  74:     final picker = ImagePicker();
  75:     final file = await picker.pickImage(
  76:       source: ImageSource.gallery,
  77:       imageQuality: 85,
  78:     );
  79:     if (file == null) return;
  80:     setState(() => _selectedImage = File(file.path));
  81:   }
  82: 
  83:   Future<void> _submit() async {
  84:     if (!_formKey.currentState!.validate()) return;
  85:     final rawPrice = _priceController.text.trim().replaceAll(',', '.');
  86:     final price = double.tryParse(rawPrice);
  87:     if (price == null) {
  88:       ScaffoldMessenger.of(
  89:         context,
  90:       ).showSnackBar(const SnackBar(content: Text('Preço inválido.')));
  91:       return;
  92:     }
  93:     setState(() => _isSaving = true);
  94:     try {
  95:       final actions = ref.read(productActionsProvider);
  96:       if (_editingProduct != null) {
  97:         await actions.updateProduct(
  98:           product: _editingProduct!.copyWith(
  99:             name: _nameController.text.trim(),
 100:             description: _descriptionController.text.trim(),
 101:             price: price,
 102:             category: _categoryController.text.trim(),
 103:             isActive: _isActive,
 104:             isFeatured: _isFeatured,
 105:           ),
 106:           newImageFile: _selectedImage,
 107:         );
 108:       } else {
 109:         await actions.createProduct(
 110:           name: _nameController.text,
 111:           description: _descriptionController.text,
 112:           price: price,
 113:           category: _categoryController.text,
 114:           isActive: _isActive,
 115:           isFeatured: _isFeatured,
 116:           imageFile: _selectedImage,
 117:         );
 118:       }
 119:       if (!mounted) return;
 120:       _cancelEditing();
 121:       ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
 122:         SnackBar(
 123:           content: Text(
 124:             _editingProduct != null
 125:                 ? 'Produto atualizado com sucesso.'
 126:                 : 'Produto cadastrado com sucesso.',
 127:           ),
 128:         ),
 129:       );
 130:     } catch (_) {
 131:       if (!mounted) return;
 132:       ScaffoldMessenger.of(
 133:         context,
 134:       ).showSnackBar(const SnackBar(content: Text('Erro ao salvar produto.')));
 135:     } finally {
 136:       if (mounted) setState(() => _isSaving = false);
 137:     }
 138:   }
 139: 
 140:   Future<void> _confirmDelete(ProductModel product) async {
 141:     final confirm = await showDialog<bool>(
 142:       context: context,
 143:       builder: (_) => AlertDialog(
 144:         title: const Text('Excluir produto'),
 145:         content: Text(
 146:           'Excluir "${product.name}"? Esta ação não pode ser desfeita.',
 147:         ),
 148:         actions: [
 149:           TextButton(
 150:             onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, false),
 151:             child: const Text('Cancelar'),
 152:           ),
 153:           FilledButton(
 154:             style: FilledButton.styleFrom(backgroundColor: AppColors.error),
 155:             onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, true),
 156:             child: const Text('Excluir'),
 157:           ),
 158:         ],
 159:       ),
 160:     );
 161:     if (confirm != true) return;
 162:     try {
 163:       await ref.read(productActionsProvider).deleteProduct(product.id);
 164:       if (!mounted) return;
 165:       ScaffoldMessenger.of(
 166:         context,
 167:       ).showSnackBar(const SnackBar(content: Text('Produto excluído.')));
 168:     } catch (_) {
 169:       if (!mounted) return;
 170:       ScaffoldMessenger.of(
 171:         context,
 172:       ).showSnackBar(const SnackBar(content: Text('Erro ao excluir produto.')));
 173:     }
 174:   }
 175:

 352:   Widget _buildProductTile(ProductModel product) {
 353:     final priceText = product.price.toBRL();
 354:     return Card(
 355:       child: ListTile(
 356:         leading: product.imageUrl.isNotEmpty
 357:             ? ClipRRect(
 358:                 borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(8),
 359:                 child: Image.network(
 360:                   product.imageUrl,
 361:                   width: 52,
 362:                   height: 52,
 363:                   fit: BoxFit.cover,
 364:                   cacheWidth: 104,
 365:                   errorBuilder: (_, _, _) => SizedBox(
 366:                     width: 52,
 367:                     height: 52,
 368:                     child: Image.asset('assets/images/petjoy_logo.png'),
 369:                   ),
 370:                 ),
 371:               )
 372:             : SizedBox(
 373:                 width: 52,
 374:                 height: 52,
 375:                 child: Image.asset('assets/images/petjoy_logo.png'),
 376:               ),
 377:         title: Text(product.name),
 378:         subtitle: Text('${product.category} · $priceText'),
 379:         trailing: Row(
 380:           mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
 381:           children: [
 382:             Switch(
 383:               value: product.isActive,
 384:               onChanged: (value) {
 385:                 ref
 386:                     .read(productActionsProvider)
 387:                     .setProductActive(productId: product.id, isActive: value);
 388:               },
 389:             ),
 390:             IconButton(
 391:               icon: const Icon(Icons.edit_outlined, color: AppColors.primary),
 392:               onPressed: () => _startEditing(product),
 393:             ),
 394:             IconButton(
 395:               icon: const Icon(Icons.delete_outline, color: AppColors.error),
 396:               onPressed: () => _confirmDelete(product),
 397:             ),
 398:           ],
 399:         ),
 400:       ),

   1: import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
   2: import 'package:flutter_riverpod/flutter_riverpod.dart';

   4: import '../../providers/auth_provider.dart';
   5: import '../../providers/user_provider.dart';
   6: 
   7: class AdminUsersScreen extends ConsumerWidget {
   8:   const AdminUsersScreen({super.key});
   9:   @override
  10:   Widget build(BuildContext context, WidgetRef ref) {
  11:     final currentUserAsync = ref.watch(currentUserProfileProvider);
  12:     final currentUser = currentUserAsync.value;
  13:     if (currentUser == null || !currentUser.isMaster) {
  14:       return const Scaffold(body: Center(child: Text('Acesso negado.')));
  15:     }
  16:     final usersAsync = ref.watch(allUsersProvider);
  17:     return Scaffold(
  18:       appBar: AppBar(title: const Text('Usuários')),
  19:       body: usersAsync.when(
  20:         data: (users) {
  21:           if (users.isEmpty) {
  22:             return const Center(child: Text('Nenhum usuário cadastrado.'));
  23:           }
  24:           final currentUser = currentUserAsync.value;
  25:           return ListView.builder(
  26:             itemCount: users.length,
  27:             itemBuilder: (context, index) {
  28:               final user = users[index];
  29:               final isMaster = user.isMaster;
  30:               final isCurrentUser = currentUser?.uid == user.uid;
  31:               return ListTile(
  32:                 leading: CircleAvatar(
  33:                   backgroundColor: isMaster
  34:                       ? Colors.amber
  35:                       : Colors.blueGrey.shade100,
  36:                   child: Icon(
  37:                     isMaster ? Icons.star : Icons.person_outline,
  38:                     color: isMaster ? Colors.white : Colors.blueGrey,
  39:                   ),
  40:                 ),
  41:                 title: Text(user.name.isEmpty ? '(sem nome)' : user.name),
  42:                 subtitle: Text(user.email),
  43:                 trailing: Chip(
  44:                   label: Text(isMaster ? 'Master' : 'Usuario'),
  45:                   backgroundColor: isMaster
  46:                       ? Colors.amber.shade100
  47:                       : Colors.grey.shade200,
  48:                 ),
  49:                 onTap: () => _changeRole(
  50:                   context: context,
  51:                   ref: ref,
  52:                   targetUser: user,
  53:                   isCurrentUser: isCurrentUser,
  54:                 ),
  55:               );
  56:             },
  57:           );
  58:         },
  59:         loading: () => const Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator()),
  60:         error: (_, _) =>
  61:             const Center(child: Text('Erro ao carregar usuarios.')),
  62:       ),
  63:     );
  64:   }
  65: 
  66:   Future<void> _changeRole({
  67:     required BuildContext context,
  68:     required WidgetRef ref,
  69:     required UserModel targetUser,
  70:     required bool isCurrentUser,
  71:   }) async {
  72:     final repository = ref.read(userRepositoryProvider);
  73:     final currentRole = targetUser.role;
  74:     final newRole = currentRole == 'master' ? 'user' : 'master';
  75:     if (currentRole == 'master' && isCurrentUser) {
  76:       ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
  77:         const SnackBar(
  78:           content: Text('Você não pode rebaixar seu próprio usuário.'),
  79:         ),
  80:       );
  81:       return;
  82:     }
  83:     if (currentRole == 'master') {
  84:       final isLastMaster = await repository.isLastMaster(targetUser.uid);
  85:       if (isLastMaster) {
  86:         if (!context.mounted) {
  87:           return;
  88:         }
  89:         ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
  90:           const SnackBar(
  91:             content: Text('Não é permitido remover o último master do app.'),
  92:           ),
  93:         );
  94:         return;
  95:       }
  96:     }
  97:     if (!context.mounted) {
  98:       return;
  99:     }
 100:     final confirm = await showDialog<bool>(
 101:       context: context,
 102:       builder: (_) => AlertDialog(
 103:         title: const Text('Alterar perfil'),
 104:         content: Text(
 105:           'Alterar "${targetUser.name}" para ${newRole == "master" ? "Master" : "Usuario"}?',
 106:         ),
 107:         actions: [
 108:           TextButton(
 109:             onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, false),
 110:             child: const Text('Cancelar'),
 111:           ),
 112:           FilledButton(
 113:             onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, true),
 114:             child: const Text('Confirmar'),
 115:           ),
 116:         ],
 117:       ),
 118:     );
 119:     if (confirm != true) {
 120:       return;
 121:     }
 122:     await repository.updateRole(targetUser.uid, newRole);
 123:     if (!context.mounted) {
 124:       return;
 125:     }
 126:     ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
 127:       const SnackBar(content: Text('Perfil atualizado com sucesso.')),
 128:     );
 129:   }
 130: }

  16: }
  17: class _CartScreenState extends ConsumerState<CartScreen> {
  18:   bool _isCheckingOut = false;
  19:   Future<void> _handleCheckout() async {
  20:     final authState = ref.read(authStateProvider);
  21:     final isAuthenticated = authState.when(
  22:       data: (user) => user != null,
  23:       loading: () => false,
  24:       error: (_, _) => false,
  25:     );
  26:     if (!isAuthenticated) {
  27:       Navigator.push(
  28:         context,
  29:         MaterialPageRoute(builder: (_) => const AuthScreen()),
  30:       );
  31:       return;
  32:     }
  33:     final userProfile = ref.read(currentUserProfileProvider).value;
  34:     if (userProfile == null) {
  35:       ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
  36:         const SnackBar(
  37:           content: Text('Erro ao carregar dados do usuário. Tente novamente.'),
  38:         ),
  39:       );
  40:       return;
  41:     }
  42:     setState(() => _isCheckingOut = true);
  43:     try {
  44:       final cart = ref.read(cartProvider);
  45:       final actions = ref.read(orderActionsProvider);
  46:       final pixData = await actions.placeOrderWithPix(
  47:         customerId: userProfile.uid,
  48:         customerName: userProfile.name,
  49:         customerEmail: userProfile.email,
  50:         items: cart.items,
  51:       );
  52:       ref.read(cartProvider.notifier).clear();
  53:       if (!mounted) return;
  54:       Navigator.of(context).push(
  55:         MaterialPageRoute(
  56:           builder: (_) => PixPaymentScreen(pixData: pixData),
  57:         ),
  58:       );
  59:     } catch (e) {
  60:       if (!mounted) return;
  61:       ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
  62:         SnackBar(
  63:           content: Text(e.toString().replaceAll('Exception: ', '')),
  64:         ),
  65:       );
  66:     } finally {
  67:       if (mounted) setState(() => _isCheckingOut = false);
  68:     }
  69:   }

  71:     final confirm = await showDialog<bool>(
  72:       context: context,
  73:       builder: (_) => AlertDialog(
  74:         title: const Text('Limpar carrinho'),
  75:         content: const Text('Remover todos os itens do carrinho?'),
  76:         actions: [
  77:           TextButton(
  78:             onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, false),
  79:             child: const Text('Cancelar'),
  80:           ),
  81:           FilledButton(
  82:             onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, true),
  83:             child: const Text('Limpar'),
  84:           ),
  85:         ],
  86:       ),
  87:     );
  88:     if (confirm == true) {
  89:       ref.read(cartProvider.notifier).clear();
  90:     }
  91:   }
  92:   @override
  93:   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
  94:     final cart = ref.watch(cartProvider);
  95:     final authState = ref.watch(authStateProvider);
  96:     final isAuthenticated = authState.when(
  97:       data: (user) => user != null,
  98:       loading: () => false,
  99:       error: (_, _) => false,
 100:     );
 101:     return Scaffold(

  12: class PixPaymentScreen extends ConsumerStatefulWidget {
  13:   const PixPaymentScreen({
  14:     super.key,
  15:     required this.pixData,
  16:   });
  17:   final PixPaymentData pixData;
  18:   @override
  19:   ConsumerState<PixPaymentScreen> createState() => _PixPaymentScreenState();
  20: }
  21: class _PixPaymentScreenState extends ConsumerState<PixPaymentScreen> {
  22:   bool _copied = false;
  23:   bool _paid = false;
  24:   @override
  25:   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
  26:     // Observa o pedido em tempo real
  27:     final orderAsync =
  28:         ref.watch(orderStreamProvider(widget.pixData.orderId));
  29:     // Detecta pagamento confirmado
  30:     orderAsync.whenData((order) {
  31:       if (order != null && order.isPaid && !_paid) {
  32:         _paid = true;
  33:         WidgetsBinding.instance.addPostFrameCallback((_) {
  34:           _showSuccessAndNavigate(order);
  35:         });
  36:       }
  37:     });
  38:     return PopScope(
  39:       canPop: false,
  40:       onPopInvokedWithResult: (didPop, _) async {
  41:         if (didPop) return;
  42:         final confirm = await _confirmCancel(context);
  43:         if (confirm == true && context.mounted) {
  44:           Navigator.of(context).popUntil((route) => route.isFirst);
  45:         }
  46:       },
  47:       child: Scaffold(
  48:         appBar: AppBar(
  49:           title: const Text('Pagar com Pix'),
  50:           automaticallyImplyLeading: false,
  51:           actions: [
  52:             TextButton(
  53:               onPressed: () async {
  54:                 final confirm = await _confirmCancel(context);
  55:                 if (confirm == true && context.mounted) {
  56:                   Navigator.of(context).popUntil((route) => route.isFirst);
  57:                 }
  58:               },
  59:               child: const Text(
  60:                 'Cancelar',
  61:                 style: TextStyle(color: AppColors.white),
  62:               ),
  63:             ),
  64:           ],
  65:         ),
