  67:           padding: const EdgeInsets.all(24),
  68:           child: Column(
  69:             crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.stretch,
  70:             children: [
  71:               // Valor
  72:               _TotalCard(
  73:                 total: orderAsync.maybeWhen(
  74:                   data: (o) => o?.total ?? 0,
  75:                   orElse: () => 0,
  76:                 ),
  77:               ),

  93:                       ),

 168:   Future<void> _copiarCodigo() async {
 169:     await Clipboard.setData(ClipboardData(text: widget.pixData.pixCode));
 170:     setState(() => _copied = true);
 171:     Future.delayed(const Duration(seconds: 3), () {
 172:       if (mounted) setState(() => _copied = false);
 173:     });
 174:   }
 175:   Future<bool?> _confirmCancel(BuildContext context) {
 176:     return showDialog<bool>(
 177:       context: context,
 178:       builder: (_) => AlertDialog(
 179:         title: const Text('Cancelar pagamento?'),

 181:           'Se sair agora o pedido ficará como "Aguardando pagamento". '

 186:             onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, false),
 187:             child: const Text('Continuar pagando'),

 189:           FilledButton(
 190:             style: FilledButton.styleFrom(
 191:               backgroundColor: AppColors.error,
 192:             ),
 193:             onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, true),
 194:             child: const Text('Sair'),
 195:           ),
 196:         ],
 197:       ),
 198:     );
 199:   }
 200:   void _showSuccessAndNavigate(OrderModel order) {
 201:     // Fecha o diálogo de espera e navega para a tela de confirmação
 202:     Navigator.of(context).pushAndRemoveUntil(

 205:           orderId: order.id,
 206:           order: order,
 207:         ),
 208:       ),
 209:       (route) => route.isFirst,
 210:     );
 211:   }

 295: class _WaitingIndicator extends StatelessWidget {
 296:   const _WaitingIndicator({required this.orderAsync});
 297:   final AsyncValue<OrderModel?> orderAsync;
 298:   @override
 299:   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
 300:     final status = orderAsync.maybeWhen(
 301:       data: (o) => o?.orderStatus,
 302:       orElse: () => null,
 303:     );
 304:     final isPaid = status != null &&
 305:         status != OrderStatus.awaitingPayment &&
 306:         status != OrderStatus.cancelled;
 307:     if (isPaid) {
 308:       return const Row(
 309:         mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
 310:         children: [
 311:           Icon(Icons.check_circle, color: AppColors.success),
 312:           SizedBox(width: 8),
 313:           Text(
 314:             'Pagamento confirmado!',
 315:             style: TextStyle(
 316:               color: AppColors.success,
 317:               fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
 318:             ),
 319:           ),
 320:         ],
 321:       );
 322:     }
 323:     return const Row(
 324:       mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
 325:       children: [
 326:         SizedBox(
 327:           width: 18,
 328:           height: 18,
 329:           child: CircularProgressIndicator(strokeWidth: 2),
 330:         ),
 331:         SizedBox(width: 10),
 332:         Text(
 333:           'Aguardando confirmação do pagamento...',
 334:           style: TextStyle(color: AppColors.grey600, fontSize: 13),
 335:         ),
 336:       ],
 337:     );
 338:   }
 339: }

   1: import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
   2: import 'package:flutter_riverpod/flutter_riverpod.dart';
   3: import '../../../core/constants/app_colors.dart';
   4: import '../../../data/models/product_model.dart';
   5: import '../../providers/cart_provider.dart';
   6: import '../../providers/product_provider.dart';
   7: import '../../widgets/product_card.dart';
   8: import '../cart/cart_screen.dart';
   9: import 'product_detail_screen.dart';
  10: class ProductListScreen extends ConsumerStatefulWidget {
  11:   const ProductListScreen({super.key});
  12:   @override
  13:   ConsumerState<ProductListScreen> createState() => _ProductListScreenState();
  14: }
  15: class _ProductListScreenState extends ConsumerState<ProductListScreen> {
  16:   final _searchController = TextEditingController();
  17:   final _scrollController = ScrollController();
  18:   String _searchQuery = '';
  19:   String? _selectedCategory;
  20:   // Ordem fixa das categorias
  21:   static const _categoryOrder = ['Cachorro', 'Gato', 'Ambos'];
  22:   @override
  23:   void initState() {
  24:     super.initState();
  25:     _scrollController.addListener(_onScroll);
  26:   }
  27:   @override
  28:   void dispose() {
  29:     _searchController.dispose();
  30:     _scrollController
  31:       ..removeListener(_onScroll)
  32:       ..dispose();
  33:     super.dispose();
  34:   }
  35:   void _onScroll() {
  36:     if (_scrollController.position.pixels >=
  37:         _scrollController.position.maxScrollExtent - 300) {
  38:       ref.read(productPaginationProvider.notifier).loadMore();
  39:     }
  40:   }
  41:   // Retorna o peso de ordenação: Cachorro=0, Gato=1, Ambos=2, outros=3
  42:   int _categoryWeight(String category) {
  43:     final idx = _categoryOrder.indexWhere(
  44:       (c) => c.toLowerCase() == category.toLowerCase(),
  45:     );
  46:     return idx >= 0 ? idx : _categoryOrder.length;
  47:   }
  48:   List<ProductModel> _applyFilters(List<ProductModel> products) {
  49:     var filtered = products;
  50:     if (_selectedCategory != null) {
  51:       filtered = filtered
  52:           .where((p) =>
  53:               p.category.toLowerCase() == _selectedCategory!.toLowerCase())
  54:           .toList();
  55:     }
  56:     if (_searchQuery.isNotEmpty) {
  57:       final query = _searchQuery.toLowerCase();
  58:       filtered = filtered
  59:           .where(
  60:             (p) =>
  61:                 p.name.toLowerCase().contains(query) ||
  62:                 p.category.toLowerCase().contains(query),
  63:           )
  64:           .toList();
  65:     }
  66:     // Ordena: Cachorro → Gato → Ambos → outros; dentro de cada grupo por nome
  67:     filtered.sort((a, b) {
  68:       final weightA = _categoryWeight(a.category);
  69:       final weightB = _categoryWeight(b.category);
  70:       if (weightA != weightB) return weightA.compareTo(weightB);
  71:       return a.name.compareTo(b.name);
  72:     });
  73:     return filtered;
  74:   }
  75:   // Retorna categorias presentes na ordem fixa
  76:   List<String> _extractCategories(List<ProductModel> products) {
  77:     final present = products
  78:         .map((p) => p.category)
  79:         .where((c) => c.isNotEmpty)
  80:         .toSet();
  81:     // Mantém a ordem fixa, adiciona categorias desconhecidas no final
  82:     final ordered = _categoryOrder.where((c) => present.contains(c)).toList();
  83:     for (final c in present) {
  84:       if (!ordered.contains(c)) ordered.add(c);
  85:     }
  86:     return ordered;
  87:   }
  88:   // "Ambos" → "Cachorro & Gato" no chip
  89:   String _chipLabel(String category) {
  90:     if (category.toLowerCase() == 'ambos') return 'Cachorro & Gato';
  91:     return category;
  92:   }
  93:   @override
  94:   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
  95:     final pageState = ref.watch(productPaginationProvider);
  96:     final cartCount = ref.watch(cartProvider).totalItems;
  97:     return Scaffold(
  98:       appBar: AppBar(
  99:         title: const Text('Produtos'),
 100:         actions: [
 101:           Badge(
 102:             label: Text('$cartCount'),
 103:             isLabelVisible: cartCount > 0,
 104:             child: IconButton(
 105:               icon: const Icon(Icons.shopping_cart_outlined),
 106:               onPressed: () {
 107:                 Navigator.push(
 108:                   context,
 109:                   MaterialPageRoute(builder: (_) => const CartScreen()),
 110:                 );
 111:               },
 112:             ),
 113:           ),
 114:         ],
 115:       ),
 116:       body: RefreshIndicator(
 117:         onRefresh: () =>
 118:             ref.read(productPaginationProvider.notifier).fetchFirst(),
 119:         child: Builder(
 120:           builder: (context) {
 121:             if (pageState.isLoading && pageState.products.isEmpty) {
 122:               return const Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator());
 123:             }
 124:             if (pageState.error != null && pageState.products.isEmpty) {
 125:               return Center(
 126:                 child: Column(
 127:                   mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
 128:                   children: [
 129:                     const Icon(Icons.error_outline,
 130:                         size: 48, color: AppColors.error),
 131:                     const SizedBox(height: 12),
 132:                     const Text('Erro ao carregar produtos.'),
 133:                     const SizedBox(height: 12),
 134:                     FilledButton(
 135:                       onPressed: () => ref
 136:                           .read(productPaginationProvider.notifier)
 137:                           .fetchFirst(),
 138:                       child: const Text('Tentar novamente'),
 139:                     ),
 140:                   ],
 141:                 ),
 142:               );
 143:             }
 144:             final categories = _extractCategories(pageState.products);
 145:             final filtered = _applyFilters(pageState.products);
 146:             return Column(
 147:               children: [
 148:                 // Barra de busca
 149:                 Padding(
 150:                   padding: const EdgeInsets.fromLTRB(12, 12, 12, 0),
 151:                   child: TextField(
 152:                     controller: _searchController,
 153:                     onChanged: (value) =>
 154:                         setState(() => _searchQuery = value.trim()),
 155:                     decoration: InputDecoration(
 156:                       hintText: 'Buscar produto...',
 157:                       prefixIcon: const Icon(Icons.search),
 158:                       suffixIcon: _searchQuery.isNotEmpty
 159:                           ? IconButton(
 160:                               icon: const Icon(Icons.clear),
 161:                               onPressed: () {
 162:                                 _searchController.clear();
 163:                                 setState(() => _searchQuery = '');
 164:                               },
 165:                             )
 166:                           : null,
 167:                     ),
 168:                   ),
 169:                 ),
 170:                 // Chips de categoria
 171:                 if (categories.isNotEmpty)
 172:                   SizedBox(
 173:                     height: 48,
 174:                     child: ListView.separated(
 175:                       padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(
 176:                           horizontal: 12, vertical: 8),
 177:                       scrollDirection: Axis.horizontal,
 178:                       itemCount: categories.length + 1,
 179:                       separatorBuilder: (_, _) => const SizedBox(width: 8),
 180:                       itemBuilder: (context, index) {
 181:                         if (index == 0) {
 182:                           final isAll = _selectedCategory == null;
 183:                           return FilterChip(
 184:                             label: const Text('Todos'),
 185:                             selected: isAll,
 186:                             onSelected: (_) =>
 187:                                 setState(() => _selectedCategory = null),
 188:                             selectedColor:
 189:                                 AppColors.primary.withValues(alpha: 0.15),
 190:                             checkmarkColor: AppColors.primary,
 191:                             labelStyle: TextStyle(
 192:                               color: isAll
 193:                                   ? AppColors.primary
 194:                                   : AppColors.grey700,
 195:                               fontWeight: isAll
 196:                                   ? FontWeight.w600
 197:                                   : FontWeight.normal,
 198:                             ),
 199:                           );
 200:                         }
 201:                         final category = categories[index - 1];
 202:                         final isSelected = _selectedCategory == category;
 203:                         return FilterChip(
 204:                           label: Text(_chipLabel(category)),
 205:                           selected: isSelected,
 206:                           onSelected: (_) => setState(() {
 207:                             _selectedCategory = isSelected ? null : category;
 208:                           }),
 209:                           selectedColor:
 210:                               AppColors.primary.withValues(alpha: 0.15),
 211:                           checkmarkColor: AppColors.primary,
 212:                           labelStyle: TextStyle(
 213:                             color: isSelected
 214:                                 ? AppColors.primary
 215:                                 : AppColors.grey700,
 216:                             fontWeight: isSelected
 217:                                 ? FontWeight.w600
 218:                                 : FontWeight.normal,
 219:                           ),
 220:                         );
 221:                       },
 222:                     ),
 223:                   ),
 224:                 // Grade de produtos
 225:                 Expanded(
 226:                   child: filtered.isEmpty
 227:                       ? Center(
 228:                           child: Column(
 229:                             mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
 230:                             children: [
 231:                               const Icon(Icons.search_off,
 232:                                   size: 48, color: AppColors.grey400),
 233:                               const SizedBox(height: 12),
 234:                               Text(
 235:                                 _searchQuery.isNotEmpty ||
 236:                                         _selectedCategory != null
 237:                                     ? 'Nenhum produto encontrado.'
 238:                                     : 'Nenhum produto disponível.',
 239:                                 style: const TextStyle(
 240:                                     color: AppColors.grey600),
 241:                               ),
 242:                             ],
 243:                           ),
 244:                         )
 245:                       : GridView.builder(
 246:                           controller: _scrollController,
 247:                           padding: const EdgeInsets.all(12),
 248:                           itemCount: filtered.length +
 249:                               (pageState.isLoading && pageState.products.isNotEmpty
 250:                                   ? 1  // spinner de carregamento
 251:                                   : (!pageState.hasMore && pageState.products.isNotEmpty
 252:                                       ? 1  // indicador de fim de lista
 253:                                       : 0)),
 254:                           gridDelegate:
 255:                               const SliverGridDelegateWithFixedCrossAxisCount(
 256:                             crossAxisCount: 2,
 257:                             mainAxisSpacing: 12,
 258:                             crossAxisSpacing: 12,
 259:                             childAspectRatio: 0.68,
 260:                           ),
 261:                           itemBuilder: (context, index) {
 262:                             if (index == filtered.length) {
 263:                               if (pageState.isLoading) {
 264:                                 return const Center(
 265:                                   child: Padding(
 266:                                     padding: EdgeInsets.all(16),
 267:                                     child: CircularProgressIndicator(),
 268:                                   ),
 269:                                 );
 270:                               }
 271:                               // Fim da lista
 272:                               return Center(

   1: import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
   2: import '../../core/constants/app_colors.dart';
   3: import '../../data/models/product_model.dart';
   4: import '../../core/extensions/format_extensions.dart';
   5: class ProductCard extends StatelessWidget {
   6:   const ProductCard({
   7:     super.key,
   8:     required this.product,
   9:     this.onTap,
  10:   });
  11:   final ProductModel product;
  12:   final VoidCallback? onTap;
  13:   // Extrai "250g" de "Embalagem: 250g"
  14:   String _parseQuantidade(String description) {
  15:     if (description.isEmpty) return '';
  16:     final parts = description.split(':');
  17:     if (parts.length < 2) return description.trim();
  18:     return parts.last.trim();
  19:   }
  20:   // "Ambos" → "Cachorro & Gato"
  21:   String _labelCategoria(String category) {
  22:     if (category.toLowerCase() == 'ambos') return 'Cachorro & Gato';
  23:     return category;
  24:   }
  25:   @override
  26:   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
  27:     final priceText = product.price.toBRL();
  28:     final quantidade = _parseQuantidade(product.description);
  29:     final categoriaLabel = _labelCategoria(product.category);
  30:     return Card(
  31:       clipBehavior: Clip.antiAlias,
  32:       child: InkWell(
  33:         onTap: onTap,
  34:         child: Column(
  35:           crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
  36:           children: [
  37:             Expanded(
  38:               child: product.imageUrl.isNotEmpty
  39:                   ? Image.network(
  40:                       product.imageUrl,
  41:                       width: double.infinity,
  42:                       fit: BoxFit.cover,
  43:                       cacheWidth: 400,
  44:                       errorBuilder: (_, _, _) {
  45:                         return const _ProductPlaceholder();
  46:                       },
  47:                     )
  48:                   : const _ProductPlaceholder(),
  49:             ),
  50:             Padding(
  51:               padding: const EdgeInsets.all(12),
  52:               child: Column(
  53:                 crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
  54:                 children: [
  55:                   Text(
  56:                     product.name,
  57:                     maxLines: 2,
  58:                     overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
  59:                     style: const TextStyle(
  60:                       fontSize: 14,
  61:                       fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
  62:                     ),
  63:                   ),
  64:                   if (quantidade.isNotEmpty) ...[
  65:                     const SizedBox(height: 2),
  66:                     Text(
  67:                       quantidade,
  68:                       style: const TextStyle(
  69:                         fontSize: 12,
  70:                         color: AppColors.grey600,
  71:                       ),
  72:                     ),
  73:                   ],
  74:                   const SizedBox(height: 4),
  75:                   Text(
  76:                     categoriaLabel,
  77:                     maxLines: 1,
  78:                     overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
  79:                     style: const TextStyle(
  80:                       fontSize: 11,
  81:                       color: AppColors.grey500,
  82:                     ),
  83:                   ),
  84:                   const SizedBox(height: 6),
  85:                   Text(
  86:                     priceText,
  87:                     style: const TextStyle(
  88:                       fontSize: 15,
  89:                       fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
  90:                       color: AppColors.primary,
  91:                     ),
  92:                   ),
  93:                 ],
  94:               ),
  95:             ),
  96:           ],
  97:         ),
  98:       ),
  99:     );
 100:   }
 101: }
 102: class _ProductPlaceholder extends StatelessWidget {
 103:   const _ProductPlaceholder();
 104:   @override
 105:   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
 106:     return Container(
 107:       width: double.infinity,
 108:       color: Colors.black12,
 109:       child: Center(
 110:         child: Image.asset(
 111:           'assets/images/petjoy_logo.png',
 112:           height: 48,

 114:         ),
